href=\"https://www.crisisgroup.org/middle-east-north-africa\">Middle East &amp; North Africa</a>          </div>\n    <h1 class=\"c-page-hero__title [ u-fs36 u-fs50@l u-lh1 u-wbbw ]\"><a href=\"/middle-east-north-africa/gulf-and-arabian-peninsula/yemen/b052-instruments-pain-i-conflict-and-famine-yemen\">Instruments of Pain (I): Conflict and Famine in Yemen</a></h1>\n        <div class=\"c-page-hero__teaser [ u-ptserif u-fs18 u-fs15@m u-fs18@l u-fsi ] u-paragraph-mar u-mar-t15 u-ellipsis-6@m u-ellipsis-5@l js-ellipsis\" style=\"word-wrap: break-word; overflow: visible;\">\n      <p>\n\tWar is denying Yemenis food to eat. This special briefing, the first of four examining the famine threats there and in South Sudan, Nigeria and Somalia, urges the Saudi-led coalition not to assault Yemen’s most important port, Hodeida, and both sides to immediately resolve deadlock over the Central Bank.</p>\n    </div><!-- /.c-page-hero__teaser -->\n      </div><!-- /.c-page-hero__details -->\n</div><!-- /.c-page-hero -->\n\n\n<div
